{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
\textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (orient)                         \(\backslash\)
    \{                               \(\backslash\)
    case \hyperlink{geom_8h_adc460053ab2088d3fe74b8b90a7a1c4caf4a03ccb67c757dc1898961486ab7ea5}{POSITIVE\_ORIENTATION}:                  \(\backslash\)
        (flag).start\_states\_set = (status);             \(\backslash\)
        break;                          \(\backslash\)
    case \hyperlink{geom_8h_adc460053ab2088d3fe74b8b90a7a1c4ca0aff14ac2a0ae953ed1cb2ca745e944e}{NEGATIVE\_ORIENTATION}:                  \(\backslash\)
        (flag).end\_states\_set = (status);               \(\backslash\)
        break;                          \(\backslash\)
    case \hyperlink{geom_8h_adc460053ab2088d3fe74b8b90a7a1c4ca43d3b2d2c3efb5f4b89ea15aa5d28552}{ORIENTATION\_NOT\_SET}:                    \(\backslash\)
        screen(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"ERROR in set\_states\_set\_at\_node\_flag() macro "}  \(\backslash\)
           \textcolor{stringliteral}{"invalid orientation value\(\backslash\)n"});          \(\backslash\)
        clean\_up(\hyperlink{cdecs_8h_afccd240f973cf154952fb917c9209719a2fd6f336d08340583bd620a7f5694c90}{ERROR});                       \(\backslash\)
